DROP TABLE book;

SET LINESIZE 200;
SET PAGESIZE 200;
SET DEFINE OFF;

COLUMN bookID             FORMAT A6;
COLUMN bookTitle          FORMAT A40;
COLUMN bookImei           FORMAT A15;
COLUMN language           FORMAT A8;
COLUMN author             FORMAT A16;
COLUMN publishYear        FORMAT 9999;
COLUMN category           FORMAT A11;
COLUMN publisherName      FORMAT A24;
COLUMN publisherLocation  FORMAT A17;

CREATE TABLE book (
    bookID              VARCHAR2(6) NOT NULL,
    bookTitle           VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
    bookImei            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    language            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    author              VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    publishYear         NUMBER NOT NULL,
    category        VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    publisherName       VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    publisherLocation   VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (bookID),
    CONSTRAINT chk_bookID_format CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(bookID, '^B[0-9]{5}$'))
);
